***глупый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пый</a> (1496)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*glupъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">глупав</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">glupav</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">глу̏пав</i>/<i class="Latn mention" lang="sh">glȕpav</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">hlúpy</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">glup</i>. Non-Slavic cognates include Old Norse <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">glópr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">idiot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (confer Icelandic <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">glópur</i>). According to <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Erich_Berneker" class="extiw" title="w:Erich Berneker">Erich Berneker</a> and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christianus_Cornelius_Uhlenbeck" class="extiw" title="w:Christianus Cornelius Uhlenbeck">Uhlenbeck</a> the Slavic words were borrowed from a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span> source, which is contested by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Max_Vasmer" class="extiw" title="w:Max Vasmer">Vasmer</a>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glúpyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)глупе́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)глупе́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>silly, stupid, foolish</li>
<li>inane</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тупой.html>тупо́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">tupój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неумный.html>неу́мный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neúmnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неразумный.html>неразу́мный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nerazúmnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:безумный.html>безу́мный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bezúmnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слабоумный.html>слабоу́мный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">slaboúmnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glúpyj</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пого</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пые</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пых</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глупый.html>глу́пая</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>blockhead, dolt, numskull</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gluxój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-арь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-arʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухарь.html>глуха́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gluxárʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухарь.html>глухаря́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухарь.html>глухари́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухарь.html>глухаре́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>western capercaillie, wood grouse, mountain cock, horse-of-the-wood</li>
<li><i>(police slang)</i> a case not likely to be solved</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gluxój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухо.html>глу́хо</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glúxo</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>deafly</li>
<li>dully, vaguely, in a muffled way (<i>sound</i>)</li>
<li>voicelessly (<i>consonant</i>)</li>
<li>out-of-the-way, remotely (<i>place</i>)</li>
<li>wildly (<i>forest</i>)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́й</a> (19318)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gluxъ</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gluxój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)глу́ше</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>deaf</li>
<li>dull, vague, muffled <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">sound</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">phonology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unvoiced, voiceless <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">consonant</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звонкий.html>зво́нкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zvónkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>out-of-the-way, remote, god-forsaken <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">place</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>overgrown, wild <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">forest</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>dead-end</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gluxój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́го</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухи́е</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухи́х</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глуха́я</a></b>)

<p><b>глу<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>хо́й</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:прилагательное.html>Прилага́тельное</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:качественный.html>ка́чественное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:или.html>или</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:относительный.html>относи́тельное</a>), <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b/c'. <a href = vnd.unilang:сравнительный.html>Сравни́тельная</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:степень.html>сте́пень</a>  |  <i>глу́ше</i>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-глух-</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ой</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li>неслышащий</li>
<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">разг.</span>, <span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;">пренебр.</span>: <a href = vnd.unilang:глухарь.html>глуха́рь</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глуха́я</a> тетеря</li>
<li>нечуткий, невосприимчивый, неотзывчивый, <a href = vnd.unilang:безразличный.html>безразли́чный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:индифферентный.html>индиффере́нтный</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:непробиваемый.html>непробива́емый</a></li>
<li><a href = vnd.unilang:приглушить.html>приглушённый</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тихий.html>ти́хий</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:невнятный.html>невня́тный</a></li>
<li>—</li>

***глухомань.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глухомань.html>глухома́нь</a> (15002)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gluxój</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">remote, desolate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + an unclear suffix.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухомань.html>глухома́нь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gluxománʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухомань.html>глухома́ни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухомань.html>глухома́ни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухомань.html>глухома́ней</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>thick forest</li>
<li>wilderness, desolate place</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> backwater, podunk</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глушитель.html>глуши́тель</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glušítelʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глушитель.html>глуши́теля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глушитель.html>глуши́тели</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глушитель.html>глуши́телей</a></b>)

***глушить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глушить.html>глуши́ть</a> (12119)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gluxój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глушить.html>глуши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glušítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заглушить.html>заглуши́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stun
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:глушить.html>глуши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́бу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>glušítʹ</b> rýbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stun fish (by means of explosives)</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:оглушить.html>оглуши́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">oglušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to deafen, to damp
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:глушить.html>глуши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:радиопередача.html>радиопереда́чи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>glušítʹ</b> radioperedáči</i> ― <span class="e-translation">jam radio broadcasts</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(plants)</i> to choke</li>
<li><i>(motor, engine etc)</i> to stop
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:глушить.html>глуши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мотор.html>мото́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>glušítʹ</b> motór</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to stop the engine</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to stifle, to suppress</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to guzzle
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:глушить.html>глуши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>glušítʹ</b> vódku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to guzzle/swill vodka</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́глушить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výglušitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глыба.html>глы́ба</a> (6200)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глыба.html>глы́ба</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">glýba</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глыба.html>глы́бы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глыба.html>глы́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глыба.html>глы́б</a></b>)

<ol><li>lump, block, burr, clod</li></ol>

***глядеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a> (282)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ględěti</i>; compare <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*glę̀dati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gljadétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взглянуть.html>взгляну́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глянуть.html>гля́нуть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поглядеть.html>погляде́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to look</li>
<li>to look after, to take care of</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:смотреть.html>смотре́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">smotrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глазеть.html>глазе́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">glazétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пялиться.html>пя́литься</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pjálitʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зырить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zyritʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><b>гля<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:деть.html>де́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 5b^.     Страд. прич. <a href = vnd.unilang:отсутствовать.html>отсу́тствуют</a>.
<a href = vnd.unilang:обычно.html>Обы́чно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:форма.html>фо́рма</a> деепричастия <i><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гля́дя</a></i>. <a href = vnd.unilang:чаща.html>Ча́ще</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всего́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:употребляться.html>употребля́ется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> непереходный.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-гляд-</b>; суффикс: <b>-е</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глядеться.html>гляде́ться</a> (21988)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gljadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеться.html>гляде́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gljadétʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look, to gaze at one's reflection <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + accusative, in a mirror, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be reflected in water</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look like <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ instrumental, someone/something</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to look right
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:диван.html>дива́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеться.html>гляди́тся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ diván ne <b>gljadítsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sofa doesn't <b>look right</b> here</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глядеть.html>гляде́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gljadétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><b>гля<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:де.html>де́</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ться</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,  <a href = vnd.unilang:возвратный.html>возвра́тный</a>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 5b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-гляд-</b>; суффикс: <b>-е</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b>; постфикс: <b>-ся</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<p><b>гля́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>нуть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:глянцевый.html>гля́нцевый</a> (17520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глянец.html>гля́нец</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gljánec</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-евый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-evyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глянцевый.html>гля́нцевый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gljáncevyj</span>)

***гнать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнать.html>гнать</a> (2135)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*gъnati</i>, from Proto-Indo-European <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷʰénti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷʰen-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">fend</i>; <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">defend</i>; <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">offend</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнать.html>гнать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погнать.html>погна́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:загнать.html>загна́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to drive</li>
<li>to distill</li>
<li>to chase, to pursue</li>
<li>to speed along</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lie</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give (<i>used in the imperative to make a forceful demand</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнать.html>Гнать</a></b> is in the class of Russian concrete verbs. Its counterpart, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гонять.html>гоня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gonjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is in the class of Russian abstract verbs.</li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнать.html>гнать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gnatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гнаться.html>гна́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">gnátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:погнаться.html>погна́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">загна́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to chase, to pursue <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> someone</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:гнаться.html>гна́ться</a></b> is in the class of Russian concrete verbs. Its counterpart, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:гоняться.html>гоня́ться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gonjátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, is in the class of Russian abstract verbs.
</p>
